64:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Part III. Qwen3-VL: Native Multimodality & Reasoning"}]
65:["$","h3",null,{"children":"1. Novelty & Contribution"}]
66:["$","p",null,{"children":["As of early 2026, ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"Qwen V3"}]," marks the arrival of ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"Native Multimodality"}],", treating images and videos as interleaved tokens in a massive ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"256K-token window"}],". Its primary contribution is the ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"\"Thinking Mode\""}],"—a reasoning-enhanced edition trained via scaled reinforcement learning (RL) to perform deliberate, self-correcting reasoning before generating a response."]}]
67:["$","h3",null,{"children":"2. Architectural Summary: DeepStack & MRoPE"}]
68:["$","p",null,{"children":"Qwen V3 replaces the MLP bridge with a unified \"Omni-architecture\":"}]
69:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"DeepStack Integration"}],": Injects visual tokens from multiple intermediate layers of the ViT into the LLM to preserve multi-level abstractions."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Interleaved-MRoPE"}],": An enhanced Rotary Positional Embedding that allows for full-frequency allocation over width, height, and time, enabling superior spatial-temporal modeling."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Thinking Mode"}],": Utilizes an internal reasoning loop where the model can use tools (e.g., ",["$","code",null,{"children":"image_zoom_in_tool"}],") to verify visual details during the \"thought\" process before outputting a final answer."]}],"\n"]}]
6a:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Chosen sub-domain:"}]," ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"Ultra-long context multimodal transformers for video + document reasoning"}],"\n",["$","strong",null,{"children":"Primary paper:"}]," Qwen3-VL technical report\n",["$","strong",null,{"children":"Thesis of the audit:"}]," Qwen3-VL is a strong ",["$","em",null,{"children":"long-context multimodal reasoner"}]," enabled by (i) frequency-balanced positional encoding, (ii) multi-level cross-layer visual injection, and (iii) textual time grounding—",["$","strong",null,{"children":"but"}]," it leaves several load-bearing engineering questions unanswered (latency/FLOPs, token budgets vs resolution, fusion alignment details), and it does ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"not"}]," close the semantic→motor gap required for robotics-grade physicality."]}]
6b:["$","hr",null,{}]
6c:["$","h2",null,{"children":"0. Problem Domain & Why It Matters"}]
6d:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Problem:"}]," Build a ",["$","em",null,{"children":"single"}]," autoregressive multimodal model that can reason over ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"interleaved text+images+video"}]," at ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"256K tokens"}]," natively, and extrapolate to ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"~1M tokens"}]," (~2h video) without catastrophic decay in temporal localization, document retrieval, or language performance.\nQwen3-VL explicitly frames \"maintaining strong pure-text capabilities\" as part of the goal."]}]
6e:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Why it’s hard (first principles):"}]}]
6f:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Long context"}]," amplifies compute cost and attention memory."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Video"}]," adds a time axis → positional encoding becomes a failure point."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Vision tokens"}]," can drown the LLM, both compute-wise and representationally (information bottleneck)."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Temporal grounding"}]," tends to become either (a) positional-ID hacks that don’t extrapolate, or (b) symbolic tokens that don’t preserve continuous dynamics."]}],"\n"]}]
70:["$","hr",null,{}]
71:["$","p",null,{"children":"We can classify long-context multimodal systems along four axes:"}]
72:["$","h3",null,{"children":"1.1 Positional encoding for space–time (t,h,w)"}]
73:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Camp A: Factorized rotary encoding (MRoPE-style)."}],"\nClassic MRoPE partitions embedding dimensions into temporal/spatial subspaces.\nQwen3-VL claims this creates an ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"imbalanced frequency spectrum"}]," that degrades long-video understanding."]}]
74:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Camp B: Frequency-balanced / interleaved rotary."}],"\nQwen3-VL’s ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"Interleaved MRoPE"}]," interleaves the t/h/w components across embedding dimensions so each axis spans both low and high frequencies."]}]
75:["$","h3",null,{"children":"1.2 Fusion mechanism: how vision enters the LLM"}]
76:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Camp A: Single-shot prefix (all visual tokens at the front)."}],"\nSimple but often shallow (one-time conditioning), and can be expensive."]}]
77:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Camp B: Cross-layer injection (DeepStack-like)."}],"\nQwen3-VL injects visual tokens into multiple early LLM layers, using intermediate vision features from multiple levels."]}]
78:["$","h3",null,{"children":"1.3 Temporal grounding strategy for video"}]
79:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Camp A: Time-synchronized positional IDs."}],"\nQwen3-VL argues this yields ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"large and sparse temporal position IDs"}]," for long videos, and requires heavy fps-diverse sampling, raising data construction cost."]}]
7a:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Camp B: Textual time tokens."}],"\nQwen3-VL adopts timestamp tokens like ",["$","code",null,{"children":"&lt;3.0 seconds&gt;"}]," and also trains with HMS formats."]}]
7b:["$","h3",null,{"children":"1.4 Long-context training"}]
7c:["$","p",null,{"children":"Qwen3-VL uses staged context growth and a curriculum that mixes 32K and 256K inputs; long-context includes “entire textbooks” and “videos up to two hours.”"}]
